{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_php_office_1_1_php_spreadsheet_1_1_worksheet_1_1_worksheet_a8d8a4add9c32a5f6416642a931a67517} 
Php\+Office\textbackslash{}\+Php\+Spreadsheet\textbackslash{}\+Worksheet\textbackslash{}\+Worksheet\+::freeze\+Pane (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$cell}{, }\item[{}]{\$top\+Left\+Cell}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Freeze Pane.

Examples\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}- A2 will freeze the rows above cell A2 (i.e row 1)
- B1 will freeze the columns to the left of cell B1 (i.e column A)
- B2 will freeze the rows above and to the left of cell B2 (i.e row 1 and column A)
\end{DoxyVerb}



\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
null | string & {\em \$cell} & Position of the split \\
\hline
null | string & {\em \$top\+Left\+Cell} & default position of the right bottom pane\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
